var isIdle = false;
var refreshIterator = 1;

jQuery.idleTimer(59000);

jQuery(document).bind("idle.idleTimer", function(){
	isIdle = true;
	//console.log('is idle')
});

jQuery(document).bind("active.idleTimer", function(){
	isIdle = false;
	//console.log('is active')
});

// this part is for the gui
function doRefresh() {
    var AMPTManager = window.AMPTManager || {};
    if (!isIdle &amp;&amp; typeof AMPTManager.refreshAllAds === 'function') {
        AMPTManager.refreshAllAds();
        refreshIterator += 1;
    }
}

jQuery(document).ready(function() {
	window.setInterval(doRefresh, 90000);
})


var RandomNumber = {
	generate: function() {
		var num = 0;
		num = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000000);
		return num;
	}
}

                                  <img alt="The image http://www.kili-no-fansub.com/images/Death_Note_logo.JPG cannot be displayed, because it contains errors." src="http://www.kili-no-fansub.com/images/Death_Note_logo.JPG"/>

                                <br/>
                                <div align="center">
                                 <br/>
                                 <font face="Verdana">
                                  <b>
                                   You heard it here first, folks.
                                   <br/>
                                   The new anime is indeed Death Note as a lot of you have speculated.
                                   <br/>
                                   This is a great show and we're proud to present it on air as well as online.
                                   <br/>
                                   It's first scheduled showing is Oct 20th at 12:00 a.m. so please don't miss it or you may find your name in a place you don't want it to be.
                                  </b>
                                 </font>
